A grand, fantasy-inspired castle with these key features:

Five main towers - two large outer towers, two medium inner towers, and one central tower
Tower roofs made of a gradient from dark oak planks at the base to magenta wool or concrete at the top, forming steep, pointed spires
Main walls constructed of light gray stone bricks
Ornate windows made of orange stained glass and item frames
A symmetrical design with the central tower being the tallest and most elaborate
Decorative elements using gold blocks, creating intricate patterns on the facades
A large, circular stained glass window in the central tower
Small turrets or pinnacles adorning the tops of each tower
Arched entrances at the base of each tower
Balconies or walkways connecting the towers
Foundation made of darker stone bricks, creating a fortified base
A central interior space with a massive, tree-like structure made of various colored glass blocks (yellow, orange, green) emanating from the center
Interior pillars made of dark oak logs
Interior flooring featuring a mix of wood planks and stone
Exterior landscaping with a patterned pathway leading to the entrance

Provide step-by-step instructions on how to construct this elaborate castle, including exact dimensions for each tower, block types for different sections, and placement of decorative elements. Describe the intricate roof design, detailing how to create the gradient effect and the pointed spires. Explain how to craft the ornate windows and the central circular window. Include instructions for the connecting elements between towers and any additional detailing visible in the images.
For the interior, provide detailed instructions on creating the central glass structure, including the color patterns and how to achieve the tree-like appearance. Describe the placement of interior pillars, flooring patterns, and any visible furnishings or decorations.
Ensure the description captures the fantasy-like, majestic appearance of the structure from both the exterior and interior perspectives. Include guidance on landscaping and pathways surrounding the castle to complete the scene.
